puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient; puis cure ceu d'oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu'il soit sanez;
then administer the treatment that generates pus, until the ties fall; then treat this with ointment suitable for this, until it is healed;

et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l'aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l'aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait .i. fil double, si que tu le trais de l'autre costeit;
and if the abscess is for the cut of the vein, it is necessary that you hold in your hand what you can of the abscess with all the skin, then push the needle under the place that you hold in your hand, and make it pierce, and there should be a double thread, so that you pull it from the other side;

puis lie l'aposteme, si com je t'ai dit, ou liien de l'une de .ij. pars as .ij. chiés dou fil;
then tie the abscess, as I have told you, or tie one of two parts at the two ends of the thread;

et se tu doutes que li filz n'isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout .i. fil desoz tout l'aposteme a l'incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en .iiij. leus;
and if you doubt that the thread will come out, push back another needle with a thread under all the abscess at the incision of the first needle, and tighten the threads in four places;

puis cope l'aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;
then cut the abscess so that the excess comes out, then cut the excess of the skin and leave what is tied;

puis met sus .i. drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d'oignemens tant qu'il soit sanez.
then put on a cloth soaked in wine and oil, then administer treatments of tents and ointments until it is healed.

des apostemes des ners
On abscesses of the nerves

Ausi com aposteme vienent en l'artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.
Just as abscesses come in the artery and in the vein, abscesses come to the nerves when they are struck, or by too great work, and similar things.

Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c'est .i. grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;
And this happens more often to the helpers and to the fingers and in all places where there are joints, and it is a grievous abscess, and its color resembles the color of the body, and is in several dispositions without pain;

et quant on l'estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n'est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;
and when one tightens it strongly, the patient feels pain, and it is not deep in the body, but under the skin;

et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer: par aventure i vanroit contraction;
and it moves well from all sides, and does not go forward or backward, nor below nor above, and that which is in joints should not be cut by iron: by chance contraction would come there;

et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.
and that which is on the head or on the forehead, split the skin with the spatula.

Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine; et s'il est grans, si le sospent a l'oncine, et l'escorche, puis l'oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu'il soit sanez.
If the abscess is small, hold it with tweezers, and cut it at its root; and if it is large, suspend it with the hook, and skin it, then remove it and bring together the wound with suture, and treat it until it is healed.

des grosses boces pendans
On large hanging lumps

Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d'aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;
Sometimes it happens in bellies and not elsewhere thelul, and it is a disease which is called "fungus" by the resemblance to them, and the root is thin, and the head large;

et en i a de petis et de mout grans; et je vis .i. home qui en avoit .ij. ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n'i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.
And there are small ones and very large ones; and I saw a man who had two on his belly that were more similar to fungi than to anything else, and there was no difference, and they were white, and had thin roots, and were already split, and moisture was always running from them.

Je les copai et trovai en l'un .xviij. onces pesant, et en l'autre .vj. З., et li ovraiges en l'incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l'artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;
I cut them and found in one 18 ounces in weight, and in the other 6 З., and the procedure in the incision is that you look if the patient is moist, and the color of the artelul is white and moist and of thin root;

si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.
so cut it with a wide spatula, and have the cautery irons in your presence at the fire.

Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;
For in cutting there often comes too great a flow of blood, and if the blood overcomes you, then hurry to cauterize;

et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l'incision dou fer, si prent .i. fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l'artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse .ij. jors;
and if you see the patient frightened and fearful of the incision of the iron, take a well-made lead thread, and tie the artelul as we have said, and leave it for 2 days;

et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d'estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu'il cope l'artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;
and then tighten it, and do not stop tightening the lead thread until it cuts the artelul, and it falls off by itself without effort;

et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu'il ne reviegne;
and if the roots are thick, there is fear in cutting especially for the belly, but you can well cut half of it, then cauterize it so that it does not come back;

puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.
then treat the wound, and be careful not to cut the thelul which is of dark color and of poor sense and of ugly appearance.

Car c'est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.
For it is a cancerous abscess, and I will come to the treatment of cancer hereafter.

quant li boude ist fuer
When the hernia comes out

Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d'arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;
If the appearance of the hernia comes by cautery of wound or by split of syfac, and is on the belly and some of the intestines come out of it, as happens in other ruptures, or from blood that runs from veins or arteries according to what is before, or from windiness;

et se c'est par la routure dou syfac et par l'issue dou bouel, si est li color de l'aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.
and if it is by the rupture of the syfac and by the exit of the bowel, the color of the abscess is similar to the color of the body, and is a light thing without pain, and appears of diverse exit.

Et se c'est por l'issue de l'intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l'entree dou bain et por fort travail.
And if it is for the exit of the intestine, then it is more diverse, and when one presses it with one's fingers it hides, and then comes back, and by chance it is closed, and grows much at the entrance of the bath and for hard work.

Et se c'est por moistor, c'est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;
And if it is for moisture, it is a light thing, and appears well when you press it with your hand, and does not constrain at all;

et se c'est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;
and if it is for blood, the abscess appears by these signs large and hard, and is fixed according to a quantity;

et se c'est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l'artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.
and if it is for windiness, it is soft to touch, and the procedure is that you look if the appearance is for the blood of the artery, or of the vein, or windiness.

Si covient que tu laisses la cure. Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t'ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l'artere et por la voine.
So it is necessary that you leave the treatment. For there is doubt and fear about it, as I have told you in the chapter on abscesses, for the artery and for the vein.

Et se li apparance est por l'intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu'il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d'enche tout entor la boude;
And if the appearance is for the intestine or the bowel, it is necessary that you command the patient to hold his breath, and be stretched out straight, then mark with ink all around the hernia;

puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l'aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;
then command him to lie on his back between your hands, then go around the place that you have marked with the spatula, then extend half of the abscess above with the large hook;

puis le lie entor d'un fil fort, ou d'une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;
then tie it around with a strong thread, or with a cord of strong silk firmly, and let the knot of the tie be undone;

puis oevre la moitiet de l'aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l'intestine;
then open half of the abscess extended on the tie, and push your index finger there, and look for the intestine;

se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l'intestine au defuer dou ventre;
if you find it caught by the tie, untie it, and push the intestine to the outside of the belly;

et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l'oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;
and if you find the bowel, take it with the hook, and cut off the excess;

et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren .ij. aguilles, et i boute .ij. fors filz, et boute les .ij. aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;
and if the artery is contrary to you, or the vein, go gently around, then return to your work and take 2 needles, and push 2 strong threads there, and push the 2 needles around what you have made in a cross that you made pierce;

puis estrain l'aposteme en .iiij. leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu'il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;
then tighten the abscess in 4 places on the needles, and if you want, remove the needles, and leave the place until it rots, and the dead flesh falls off by itself;

ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu'il covient, et cheve l'aposteme si com nos avons dit;
or you cut it when it will be thinned and rotted, then treat it with what is necessary, and dig out the abscess as we have said;

et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu'il couvient, et soude le leu.
and extract the blood or the moisture that you find, then treat the place with what is necessary, and solder the place.

dou chancre
On cancer

Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;
We have said in the division the appearances of cancer, and how one should work on it with medicines, and how one should avoid the treatment of iron;

et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l'encomencement;
and we say the cancer engendered in the womb, and great caution in the treatment, and the ancients said that when cancer is in a place where one can scrape it as cancer which is in breasts, and in the thigh, and in similar places, and one should remove it all when it is in the beginning;

et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l'aproches, car je n'en poi onques nul saner; ne nulz n'en sana onques devant moi.
and when it is large and old, it is not necessary that you approach it, for I could never heal any; nor did anyone ever heal one before me.

Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;
And the procedure, when it is in a place where one can remove it, as we have said, is that you purge sometimes the patient of black bile;

puis le fai sainier s'il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide .i. boin leu por faire l'ovraige;
then make him bleed if he has manifest repletion, then prepare the patient a good place to do the work;

puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l'oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;
then throw your hooks into the cancer, and dig it out from all sides, and remove it from all sides without leaving anything;

et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l'incision de l'artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;
and let all the blood run out, and squeeze well the place with your hand or with something, and if the flow of blood is contrary to you from the incision of the artery or of the vein, cauterize it until the blood is stanched;

puis le cure d'autre cure tant qu'il soit sanez.
then treat it with other treatment until it is healed.

de ydropisie
On dropsy

Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d'idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l'aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer: si est eclites soulement;
We have already said in the division the appearances of dropsy, and in what manner the gathering of water is made, and the signs of each appearance, and the treatment which is done by medicines, and that which is treated by iron: so it is eclites only;

et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces .ij. semblances: c'est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c'est mortelz chose;
and one should not touch with iron in these 2 appearances: that is to say, tympanites and yposarche, for it is a mortal thing;

donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s'il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;
therefore when you treat this appearance of dropsy which is called "eclites" with medicines, and the treatment does not profit, look if the patient is weak, or if he has another illness than dropsy, such as cough and solution of belly and similar things;

si n'i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance; et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n'a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n'est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:
so do not touch with iron, for there is doubt; and if you see the patient of strong virtue, and he has no other illness than dropsy only, and he is neither too young nor too old, you should work thus:

lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l'aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:
raise the patient straight up on your hands, and the minister presses the belly pushing the water to the lowest part of the chest, then take the spiny spatula according to this form:

Et soit trenchans de .ij. pars. a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu'il puist venir jusc'a l'intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;
And let it be cutting on 2 sides. at the point, and yet not so entering that it can come to the intestine when one sticks it in, and cannot hurt it;

puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines: si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude .iij. dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;
then look if the dropsy is engendered towards the intestines: so it is necessary that you split away from the navel 3 fingers right below on the groin;

et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude .iij. dois;
and if the dropsy is for the disease of the liver, let your split be to the left of the navel 3 fingers;

et se c'est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;
and if it is for the spleen, let it be to the right, and it is not necessary that the patient lie on the split so that the superfluities do not run to that weak place;

puis perce tout le cuir a l'estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d'une ungle ou enqui entor;

Then pierce the entire skin with the instrument, and push it, and lift your hand with the spatula between the skin and the peritoneum as if skinning to the extent of a fingernail or thereabouts;

puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c'est li leus de l'aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:

Then pierce the peritoneum until the spatula reaches the empty space, which is where the water is, then pull it out, and insert this instrument of which here is the shape:

Et est semblans a une caine d'argent subtil, et est d'arain ou d'archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz .i. petit pertus; et ou costeit d'une part, .iij. pertus; et .ij. d'autre part, et .i. d'autre;

And it resembles a thin silver tube, and is made of brass or light copper, and has a small hole in the lower part; and on one side, three holes; and two on the other side, and one on another;

et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c'est li forme de l'incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:

and the tip is cut like a quill, and this is the shape of the incision with which the scribe cuts the quill:

au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l'aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l'estrument;

At the upper end is the blade, so that when the instrument reaches the water, it immediately descends onto the instrument;

vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu'il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l'arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;

Empty then half or a third part, because if you empty more than is necessary at that time, perhaps the patient dies due to the dissolution of his spirit from the soul, or he falls unconscious, or he approaches death;

mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;

but empty according to the quantity of his strength, and according to what the dispositions of the patient's strength indicate, and his pulse;

puis trai l'estrument et retien l'aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j'ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;
then pull out the instrument and retain the water, and it is now retained by the skin that blocks the hole which is on the peritoneum, of which I have spoken, that you pierce in this manner;

puis rencomence l'estrument l'autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l'aigue une petite quantiteit;
then start again with the instrument the next day, if you see the patient tolerating it, and draw a small quantity of water;

fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu'il ni demore mais c'un poc d'aigue.
Do this for a few days, and be careful not to act foolishly until there remains only a little water.

Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d'aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;
And if you have doubts about the patient, and you leave much water, treat him with hot sand burial, and by much sweating in the bath and in the sun, and let him abstain from drinking;

et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu'il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l'estomac et sus lou foie et sus l'esplen aprés l'estraction de l'aigue, si com j'ai dit devant.
and treat him with drying medicines until he is healed, and cauterize on the stomach and on the liver and on the spleen after the extraction of the water, as I have said before.

de l'estopement de la verge
On the obstruction of the penis

Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n'ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n'est mie en son leu.

Sometimes children are born who have no hole in the penis, or the hole is small, or it is not in its place.

Si le covient tantost qu'il n'aist percier a tout .i. spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:

So it is necessary to pierce it immediately after birth with a very thin spatula according to this shape:

puis met ou pertus .i. clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi .iij. jors ou iiij.

then put a thin lead nail in the hole, and tie it and keep it thus for 3 or 4 days.

et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;

and when he wants to urinate, remove the nail, let him urinate, and then put it back;

et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.

and perhaps it is not necessary, because the urine that comes out does not let it close.

Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s'eslargera.

Those whose hole is small are treated with the lead nail, as we have said, so it will widen.

Cil qui n'ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s'il ne lievent lor verge en haut;

Those who do not have the hole in its place are injured, because some are born who have the hole at the head of the penis, which is why they cannot urinate forward if they do not lift their penis up;

et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc'a la marris, et c'est une male maladie.

and they cannot procreate because the matter cannot reach the womb, and this is a bad disease.

Et li maniere de l'ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d'une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;

And the manner of the operation is that the patient lies on his back, then extend the head of the penis and cut it like the cut of a quill, so that the hole falls in the middle, as it should;

et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s'il avient, si l'estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu'il soit sanez.

and beware of the flow of blood that often comes, and if it happens, stanch it with what stanches blood, and treat the wound until it is healed.

des pustules de la verge

On pustules of the penis

Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide; et en i a malignes et non malignes;

Often these white spots come on the penis, and it is an appearance of ugly flesh; and there are malignant and non-malignant ones;

si covient que tu les preignes a .i. oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;

so it is necessary that you take them with a thin hook, and cut and clean them all, then put cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment on them;

puis le cure d'oignement diafinicon tant qu'il soit sanez.  Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.

then treat it with diafinicon ointment until it is healed.  And if the white spot is malignant, of foul color and stinking, it is necessary that you administer cautery.

Quant tu l'as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l'albathe qui est dedens premier;

When you have cut it, and if the white spot is at the tip of the penis, and has part inside the skin and part outside, it is necessary that you remove the white spot that is inside first;

et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer. Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n'est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu'il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;

and when it is healed, treat it outside. Because when you treat them together, the head of the penis is not assured that it will not be pierced, and blackness and corruption come to the tip of the penis and the testicle;

si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l'emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d'escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d'autres cures tant qu'il soit sanez.

so it is necessary to remove all that is black and corrupted, then tie on a plaster of honey and flour made from pomegranate peel and vetches, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.

Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:

And if a flow of blood comes, administer the lunar cautery according to this shape:

Li cauteres si aide as .ij. dispositions ensamble: c'est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;

The cautery helps the two conditions together: that is, the flow of blood, and the corruption;

et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;

and if the head of the penis is corrupted and retracted, it is necessary that you put a lead tube in the canal of the penis, and the patient urinates through it;

et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n'ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l'escorches a .i. estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;

and when the skin is attached to the head of the penis which happens to those who have not been circumcised, or it happens due to a wound or an abscess, it is necessary then that you scrape it with a hollow instrument, until the ligament is untied, and the head of the penis is freed from all sides;

et se c'est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l'escorches a .i. spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;

and if it is difficult to separate this, it is necessary that you scrape it with a spatula a little from the head of the penis and from the skin;

puis dessevre belement entre .ij., et i met .i. subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu'il n'aerse derechief.

then gently separate between the two, and put a thin linen cloth moistened with cold water, so that it does not reattach.

de la circoncision

On circumcision

Circoncision n'est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies; toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.

Circumcision is not a disconnection of continuity like other wounds; however, when we do this work of our own will, and properly on children, it is necessary that we do the best work, and the easiest for health.

Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n'en usent mie en lor loi, et n'en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.

I say that the ancients did not speak of the circumcision of their children, because they do not use it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired by experiment.

Car j'ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor .i. dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;

For I have seen the greatest part of the masters and the elders who performed circumcision around a scythe, and with scissors, and with a razor;

si fuioit li keurs car il i a .ij. toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.

so the skin would flee because there are two layers, and perhaps one cuts the upper one and the lower one remains.

Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n'est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;

Now it is necessary to cut it again, and the pain is double, and with the cleaning that is done with the scythe, the point of the member is not assured;

et a la mundification de l'ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l'uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu'il n'ont mestier de mundification et je l'ai veut.

and with the cleaning of the nail perhaps the iron escapes, and corrupts the work, and many times they are born so that they do not need cleaning and I have seen it.

De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l'experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.

Of the cleaning that is done with scissors with all the thread binding, I have found the goodness of the experiment, because the scissors cut just as well above as below.

Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en .i. tout soul tens; mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;

For when you press your hand, you cut equally in one single time; but let the thread be very tight around the skin;

et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l'enfant, s'il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;

and let the manner of the first work be that you make the child think, if he understands, that you are only tying the thread around the penis, and then make him rejoice in all the ways that you can;

puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;

then make him stand straight between your hands, and hide the scissors between your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see them, nor any of the instruments;

puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;

then push your hand to the penis and blow on the skin, and pull it up until the head of the penis is inside;

puis la mundifie bien de l'ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d'un fil double, puis la lie desoz .i. poc a .i. autre liien;

then clean it well of the dirt that has gathered there, then tie the marked place with a double thread, then tie it below a little with another tie;

et la tien as .ij. dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les .ij. liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;

and hold it with two fingers by the second tie at the thumb and index finger, and cut between the two ties, then quickly lift the skin above and pull the head of the penis;

puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c'est li muedres; et met poudre sus et sus la poudre .i. drapeil glueit d'un moieuf d'uef cuit destempreit d'aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc'a l'autre jor, et le cure d'autre cure tant qu'il soit sanez.

then let the blood flow little by little, for it is the best; and put powder on it and on the powder a cloth glued with a cooked egg yolk mixed with rose water, prepared with good and fresh rose oil, and leave it on until the next day, and treat it with other treatments until it is healed.

Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste: li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:

The shape of the scissors for cleaning is this: the two ends should be thin and sharp, and the ends should be as large as the handles equally:

li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l'incision; donques il covient que tu l'estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;

the error of cleaning is when the inner skin flees from the incision; then it is necessary that you extend it with your nail, before the place makes an abscess;

et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.

and cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it with your nail, hold it with pliers, and then cut it.

Et s'il trespassent .iij. jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l'escorche legierement;

And if three days pass, and what is under the penis is swollen, leave it until the hot abscess is calmed, and scrape it lightly;

si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.

cut it as best you can, and be careful of the part of the penis, it will not harm it at all.

Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s'on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;

Therefore treat the place with things that solder the wound with powder, which we have mentioned in the treatise on powders, and if one cuts the skin excessively, and it goes above, it will not harm;

cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu'il soit sanez.

treat it then, as we have said, until it is healed.

dou retenement de l'urine

On the retention of urine

Li retenue de l'urine si est d'opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;

The retention of urine is from obstruction by stone, or congealed blood, or pus, or newly grown flesh, or similar things, which we have mentioned in the division;

et se li urine n'est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;

and if the urine is not released, and you see that it is retained because of the stone which is already in the neck of the bladder, it is necessary that the patient be bent over his knees;

et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s'alainne tant com il puet;

and let his feet be put on his back, and extend his belly from the part above the back, and let the patient restrain his breath as much as he can;

et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l'expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;

and then the neck of the bladder is constrained to the expression of the stone above, which is why the urine is released;

et s'elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l'estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme: et soit d'argent subtilz legiere

and if it does not come, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, it is necessary that you administer extraction with the instrument which is called "syringe", of which here is the form: and let it be of thin light silver

chevee, si com li penne d'un oiseil; et soit li caine d'une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.

hollowed, like the feather of a bird; and let the tube be a palm and a half long, and be thin at the end.

Et li maniere de l'issue de l'urine si est que tu pren .i. fil double, et lie au chief .i. poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;

And the manner of the exit of the urine is that you take a double thread, and tie at the end a little wool or cotton, and push the end of the thread inside the syringe;

et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc'au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d'oile ou de burre et d'aubin d'uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus .i. siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d'oile moiste et d'oile d'olive et d'aigue tede;

and cut the excess of the wool and push it to the end of the syringe, then anoint the syringe with oil or butter and egg white, and make the patient sit on a seat, and sprinkle his bladder and penis with moist oil and olive oil and warm water;

puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu'elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;

then gently put the syringe in the penis, until it comes to the root of the penis, then double the penis above towards the navel;

puis boute la siringue avant jusc'a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc'a la chose vuide, et ceu n'est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;

then push the syringe forward to the bladder, and let the patient feel it come to the empty thing, and this is not done according to this order except because the passage where it goes is twisted;

puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l'estrai fuer, et fai corre l'urine;

then extend the thread with all the wool little by little, and the urine follows the wool, then pull it out, and make the urine run;

et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.

and start again with the syringe until the bladder is emptied, and let the patient be relieved.

des maladies de la vessie

On diseases of the bladder

Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l'estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c'est li forme:

When abrasions or blood come into the bladder, or pus is gathered there, and you want to distill waters and medicines, do it with the instrument which is called "clepsydra", and this is its form:

Elle est close, et si a .iij. pertus: .ij. d'une part, et .i. d'autre, si com tu vois; et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu'il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c'on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;

It is closed, and has three holes: two on one side, and one on the other, as you see; and let the hollowed place through which the medicine runs be such that it well stops the penis without addition, so that one can draw out the moisture, and push when necessary;

et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;

and when you want to throw your medicines into the bladder, put the head of the syringe in the moisture, and pull on the plunger that is inside;

si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens; si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;

so you will draw the moisture into the syringe, and then push the plunger back in strongly; so the moisture will enter in, and will come to the bladder now, so that the patient will feel it;

et c'est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie: si est ci:

and this is the form of the thin clyster with which one administers an enema to the bladder: it is here:

Et est d'argent ou d'archaut, et est li chiés plus haut; et desoz a .i. sein ou li liiens chiet;

And it is of silver or copper, and the head is higher; and below there is a bell where the tie falls;

puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les .ij. seins forment d'un boin fil double, et chaufe .i. poc celle moistor sus le feu;

then take a sheep's bladder and put in it the moisture with which you want to administer an enema to the bladder, then tie it between the two bells strongly with a good double thread, and heat that moisture a little on the fire;

puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;

then push the head of the clyster into the penis, then press your hand on the bladder with all the moisture suitably, until the patient feels that this moisture has already come to the bladder;

et se tu n'as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai .i. cercle, et le perce rondement entor;

and if you don't have the bladder, take a piece of parchment, and make a circle of it, and pierce it roundly around;

puis boute .i. fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble .i. dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d'oile et de moistor et d'aigue, et le lie en l'estrument;

then push a strong thread into these holes, then assemble the circle as one assembles a scythe, and put inside what you want of oil and moisture and water, and tie it to the instrument;

et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.

and do as you did with the bladder, pressing with your hand until the moisture comes to the bladder.



de la piere
About the stone

Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l'estraction ensamble medicines; et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille; et en la vessie, et en la verge; et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.
We have already spoken in the division about the types of stones, and the extraction along with medicines; and I have said the difference between stones generated in the kidneys, and all the signs, and on which stones one should operate by cutting; and in the bladder, and in the penis; and I will tell you about it openly and briefly.

Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c'est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit; et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist; et a mout de ces saut li fondemens; et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu'il ont .iiij. ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece; et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l'ont petite.
I say that the stone which is generated in the bladder happens more often to children, and it is a sign that the water jumps from the bladder similar to water in its subtlety; and sand appears, and the patient scratches his penis, and it hangs many times, and then hardens; and for many of these the anus prolapses; and the healing is easy for children until they are 4 years old, and is very difficult in old people, and is moderate for young people, those who are between youth and old age; and the cure is easier for those who have large stones, than for those who have small ones.

Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.
And when we come to the cure, it is necessary first to cleanse the patient by enema, to draw out all the waste that is in the intestines.

Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.
Because it sometimes hinders searching for the stone.

Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut; puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval; puis la quier et la touche dedens; se tu sens la piere en l'espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.
Then take the patient by the feet, and push and move him downwards, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes jumps from the high place; then make him sit between your prepared hands, and his hands should be under his thighs, so that the bladder is all declining downwards; then search for it and touch it inside; if you feel the stone in the space, then hasten now to cut upon the stone.

Et s'elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d'oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis; et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l'amoine au col de la vessie; puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.
And if it does not fall to the touch at all, then moisten your index finger with oil from the left hand, if the patient is a child, or your middle finger, if the patient is a completed youth; and push it into his anus, and search for the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, bring it to the neck of the bladder; then press on it with your finger, and push it outwards where you want to cut.

Et comande au ministre qu'il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu'il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille; puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:
And command the assistant to press the bladder with his hand, and command him to extend the testicles upwards with his right hand, and with his left hand remove the skin that is under the testicles in the part where one makes the cut; then push in the cutting spatula, of which this is the shape:

Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre; et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu'ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans; par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu'elle saut fuer sens travail; et saiches qu'il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges: si est griés a issir; et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.
And cut between what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the side of the left buttock; and be straight on the stone, and your finger should always be in the anus, and let the cut be transverse so that it is wide on the outside, and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large; perhaps press so with the finger that is in the anus, that it jumps out without effort; and know that there are such stones where there are angles, and margins: so it is difficult to exit; and there are such that are smooth, similar to an acorn, and round, of which the exit is easy.

A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant; et s'elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu'elle n'eschaipe; ou tu boute desoz li .i. estrument subtil corbé au chief; et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge .i. poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l'estrainche de vitriole; et s'il i a plus d'une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s'il en i a plusors.
For those therefore where there are angles and margin, make the cut larger; and if it does not jump out, it is necessary that you grip it with forceps that are like a file at the end, to better grip the stone so that it does not escape; or you push under it a subtle curved instrument at the end; and if you cannot manage it thus, then enlarge the hole a little, and if blood flows, then staunch it with vitriol; and if there is more than one stone, then push first the largest to the neck of the bladder, then cut on it, then draw it out, and the small ones after if there are several.

Et s'elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.
And if it is very large, it is necessary to saw it, and make a larger wound.

Car .ij. choses avienent au malaide: ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder; mais toutevoie t'efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces; et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d'encens et d'aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l'estraint, et met par sus .i. drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l'aposteme chaut; puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc'au tier jor.
For two things happen to the patient: either he dies, or the urine always comes through there because the place cannot heal; but nevertheless strive to extract, or to break with forceps, until you draw it out in pieces; and when you have completed your work, then fill the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, and tighten it, and put on top a cloth moistened in oil and wine, or in oil and rose water and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess; then lay the patient back on his neck, and do not untie the bandage until the third day.

Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d'oile et d'aigue, puis le cure d'oignement dyafinicon et d'oignement basilicon, tant qu'il soit sanez.
And when you untie it, then water the place well with oil and water, then treat it with diaphoenicon ointment and basilicon ointment, until it is healed.

Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l'urine: boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s'il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit; puis leve la plaie d'aigue et d'aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu'il soit sanez; et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les .ij. cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.
And if a hot abscess comes in the wound and corrosions, and congealing of blood in the bladder, and the urine is retained by this, which is known in such a way that blood jumps with the urine: then push your finger into the wound, and extract that blood, for if it remains, it will corrupt the bladder, and rot it; then wash the wound with water and vinegar and salt, and help it in all the ways that you know, until it is healed; and it is necessary that every time you treat it, that you tie the two thighs, and gather the medicines on the place.

Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.
And if the stone is small, and it is in the conduit of the penis, and stuck in there, and the urine cannot come out; then treat it with what I say before, that you cut it many times, one is excused from cutting by this treatment.

Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.
I have already proved this thus.

Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:
Take an iron drill according to this shape and let it be with three angles fixed in a stick:

puis pren .i. fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu'ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu'il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d'autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.
then take a thread and tie it around the penis below the stone, so that it cannot come back into the bladder; then push the drill into the penis lightly, until it comes to the stone; and turn the drill with your hand in the stone little by little, until you can pierce the stone on the other side; then the urine will come immediately, then press your hand on what remains of the stone that is inside the penis.

Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l'urine, et est garis li malaides; et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie .i. fil desoz la piere et .i. autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les .ij. liiens, puis l'estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu'il soit sanez.
So it is immediately broken, and jumps out with the urine, and the patient is healed; and if you cannot do this because of something that prevents it, then tie a thread below the stone and another above, then split the penis right at the stone between the two ties, then extract it, and untie the tie, and clean the congealed blood that is in the wound; and treat it until it is healed.

de la piere des femmes
About women's stones

Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s'il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l'une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c'on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.
It rarely happens that stone is generated in women, and if it happens sometimes, the cure is difficult, and is forbidden for three things: one is that perhaps the woman is a virgin; and the second is that one cannot find a woman well-knowing who reveals herself to doctors, especially when she is chaste.

Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l'ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a.
And the third manner is that perhaps one cannot find a woman well-knowing in this art of hands; and the fourth manner is that the stone of the woman is deeper than the stone of the man, for which it is necessary to make a deeper cut, and there is great fear.

Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n'en trueves, point si quier .i. caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l'art, et li comande qu'ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l'inquisicion de la piere; et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s'ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu'elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.
And if necessity calls for this, it is necessary that you take a well-knowing midwife, and one hardly finds one, and if you do not find one, then seek a subtle chaste doctor; and present to him a very wise midwife in the life of women, or a woman who knows a part of the art, and command her to do what you command her about the investigation of the stone; and look very well if the woman is a virgin: then it is necessary to push her finger into the anus and search for the stone; and if she finds it, then let her constrain it under her finger, and recommend that she push her finger into the vagina of the patient, and search and press her left hand on the bladder strongly.

S'elle la trueve, si covient qu'elle la mueve de greit en greit des l'entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu'elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne
If she finds it, it is necessary that she move it gradually from the entrance of the bladder down to below, until it comes to the root of the thigh; then cut on the stone at the root of the thigh against the middle of the vagina, where it is most accessible, and feel the stone in that part; and do not

mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite; puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c'est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains. si saiches les semblances por savoir l'issue.
move her finger above or below the stone, and let the cut be small at first; then push the probe into the cut, if you feel the stone then increase the wound until the stone can come out, and know that there are many kinds of stones: that is to say, small and large and rough and smooth, long and round, and those that have branches. So know the appearances to know the outcome.

Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t'ai dit en l'estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre; et se li sans te vaint, et c'est de l'artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l'estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.
And if the blood overcomes you, put ground vitriol on the place, and hold it for an hour until the blood is stanched; then return to your work, until the stone is out, and have the instruments that I told you about in the extraction of stones in men to help you in your work; and if the blood overcomes you, and it is from the artery that is cut, put the powder on the place and the straw of tents and bandages, and do not restart this, and leave the stone and do not draw it out, lest by chance the patient would die; then treat the wound.

Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.
And when the heat of the blood is calmed, and the place rots, then return to your work, until the stone is out.

de hernie carnouse
About fleshy hernia

Ramice aquouse n'est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l'uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l'uef, si c'on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c'est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n'avient se poc non.
Watery hernia is nothing other than a gathering of moisture in the white syfac, which is beneath the skin of the testicles, which contains the egg; and it is called "syfac", and sometimes it is properly in the membrane of the egg, so that one thinks it is another egg; and it is the skin of the testicle between the white syfac that we have mentioned; and this happens only rarely.

Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.
And the generation of this hernia is from weakness that comes to the testicles, and this matter is spread out.

Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c'est color declinans a jaunice, ou c'est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus; et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s'elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, .i. poc lonc si com li figure d'un oef, et n'apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.
And sometimes it comes from a blow to the testicles, and this moisture has many colors: either it is a color tending towards jaundice, or it is without red, or black, or watery white, and this happens more often; and these are the signs to recognize this gathering, for if it is in the white syfac that we have mentioned, then the abscess is round, a little long like the shape of an egg, and the testicles do not appear, because there is moisture all around.

Et s'il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l'uef, et por ceu pense on que c'est uns autres oef; et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l'intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant. Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l'intromiss oire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.
And if there is moisture in the proper membrane, then the abscess is round with a part of the egg, and because of this one thinks that it is another egg; and if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white syfac, one feels it well; therefore when you want to know the color of the moisture, test with the square probe, of which the shape is given before. According to what comes after the probe, judge what is inside.

Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz; puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu'il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l'un des .ij. costelz dou keur des coions; puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc'a syfac blanc, et l'escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir; puis perce lou syfac plain d'aigue a .i. large pertus, et estrai toute l'aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue; et se l'uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l'uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les .ij. leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu'il soit sanez.
And when we treat it with iron, it is necessary that the patient be bled according to his ability and the repletion of his body; then lay him on his back, on something a little high, and put many cloths under him; then sit on his left, and command the assistant to sit on the right, and extend the penis to one of the two sides of the skin of the testicles; then take the wide spatula, and cut the skin of the testicles through the middle lengthwise up to near the groin, and let your cut be straight in dividing the skin of the testicles up to the white syfac, and scrape it subtly according to your ability; then pierce the syfac full of water with a large hole, and draw out all the water, and then put your hooks, and extend the syfac upwards; and do not touch the skin of the testicles, but only the syfac; cut all or in pieces especially the subtle side of it, for if you do not cut it very wisely, the water will return; and if the egg jumps out during your work, bring it back to its place when you have completed the work on the syfac; then bring together the two lips of the skin of the testicles with a suture, then treat it like other wounds, until it is healed.

Et se tu trueves l'uef corromput d'autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l'uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.
And if you find the egg corrupted by another disease, it is necessary that you tie the vessels that are suspensory, fearing the flow of blood; then cut the testicle with all the suspensory, and extract the egg, and treat it as we have said.

Et se aigue est assemblee en .ij. parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont .ij. ramices; si cope l'autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset; et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les .ij. coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:
And if water is gathered in two parts together, know that these are two hernias; so cut the other part as you did the first equally, then dry the blood, and put in the wound wool moistened in rose oil; and put outside other wool moistened in wine and oil, and put it on the two testicles, and put doubled cloths on top, and tie it up with all the bandage which is according to this form:

Puis pren .ij. drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient
assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc'au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les .ij. angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier; et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes .i. cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l'aigue est descovers; si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l'escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:
Then take two cloths, and fill them with lint wool according to this appearance and let them be
assembled by sewing in the throat of the breeches, and one of the ends take on the anus up to the back, and the other to the part of the groin; and the other two ends on the two groins, and let all the restraint be assembled in the buckle of the breeches; and sometimes this hernia is treated with cautery instead of cutting with iron, and it is that you take a subtle knife-like cautery, and cut the skin of the testicles, and let it be heated as we have said, so that the white syfac that contains the water is uncovered; so take the cautery according to this form, and pierce that syfac with hooks, and scrape it with this subtle hot cautery:

Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l'uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille; et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.
And cut it in all the ways that you can, until you uproot everything; and make sure that the fire does not touch the egg; and know that this work is safer; and better guarding against flow of blood, and better than the work of cutting; and if anything opposes you, either hot abscess or flow of blood or other thing, then treat what opposes you, according to what was said before.

Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus .i. siege leveit; pues perce l'aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer; puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l'aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee; et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l'aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l'estrument dont on trait l'aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge .i. poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés .vj. mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.
And if the patient is fearful, and does not want to wait for this work because of its horribleness, then administer perforation, as I tell you, and it is that when you are very certain by the signs that we have said that watery hernia is there, make the patient sit on a raised seat; then pierce the abscess in the lower part with all the wide spatula, and put the perforation along the length of the body; and let the hole be wide, so that all the water runs out; then put cotton on the place, and tie it, and leave to run the remainder of the water, then treat it until the wound is healed; and if the white membrane does not let the water out at the mouth of the wound, it is necessary that you push in a feather or the instrument with which one draws the water from dropsy patients, of which the form is given before; and widen the wound a little, and know that the water returns, and is gathered after 6 months or thereabouts, and when it is gathered as before, and thus will the patient pass his days.

de l'aposteme des coions
On the abscess of the testicles

Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c'on la laisse; et je vos dirai l'ovraige et les semblances de l'aposteme.
Know that in the cutting of this hernia there is fear in several conditions, which is why it seems to me better to leave it; and I will tell you the procedure and the appearances of the abscess.

Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c'est par mout de cas.
I say then that many abscesses come to the body, and especially to the testicles; and this is due to many cases.

C'est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion; et est li color de l'aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief; et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d'artere, ou d'enfleure de voine.
That is to say by sharp and acute superfluity, which is spread to the testicles, or from percussion; and the color of the abscess is according to the color of the body; and it does not find any pain, and is a serious abscess; and by chance it is a serious, fearful and worse abscess, and of dark color, and sometimes comes from a knot of artery, or swelling of vein.

Quant c'est par nout d'artere, si est conus par la disposition d'aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois; et ne covient mie que tu i touches.
When it is by a knot of artery, it is known by the disposition of a hot abscess, when you press it with your fingers; and it is not appropriate that you touch it.

Cil qui est fais d'enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l'expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars; et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l'uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l'uef.
The one that is made from swelling of vein is known by its disposition to the expression of the touch of fingers, and one can well make the cut on this appearance, and on the other flesh; and it is that you cut the heart of the testicles, then extend the egg upwards, and pull it out of the white membrane, and deliver the suspensory from all parts of the egg.

Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l'uef, et lou cope; et s'il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.
If the egg is already soldered with these born flesh, then it is appropriate that you pull the egg, and cut it; and if it is attached to the membrane, or in that which is inside the vessels, it is appropriate that you deliver all this thin part, and cut it roundly.

Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l'uef, si com nous avons dit.
And if the birth of the flesh is in the back place, it is appropriate that you cut it all, and extract the egg, as we have said.

Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d'autres cures tant qu'il soit sanez.
And when your work is accomplished, fill the wound with wool soaked in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.


de l'aposteme des coions
On the abscess of the testicles

Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d'un envoloupement semblant a .i. borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait; et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l'ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.
This is an abscess enveloped in a wrapping similar to a bud, with the softening of the testicles, and the patient moves with difficulty when he walks; and the treatment of this disease is nearly as fearsome as the one before, and yet we will tell you its procedure, according to what the ancients did.

Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus .i. siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment; puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu'il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l'estraction des arteres qui sont en temples; puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l'autre chief; puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues; puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l'un des coions; car par ceu n'i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz; si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l'incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.
It is appropriate that you make the patient sit on a raised seat, then push the suspensory of the testicles down with your fingers, with all the vessels that are close to the penis, and the master holds them, and extends them strongly; then cut with a large cutting spatula across the vessels, until they are uncovered, and then skin each part, as we have said in the extraction of arteries that are in temples; then stick a needle with a double thread, and tie it at the first place where the screw has come, and tie it again at the other end; then cut them in the middle directly, according to the length of the body, and draw out the corrupted moisture; then treat the wound as the others where pus is generated, so that some vessels fall that nourish one of the testicles; for by this no harm comes, and if to all the vessels comes screw, it is appropriate to draw the testicles with all the vessels; so that the egg does not lose its nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, and they dry and cannot help themselves.

de la routure dou syfac
On the rupture of the membrane

Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l'estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l'un des coions; et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l'estension de li, et vienent ces .ij. manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses; et li signes quant c'est de l'estension dou syfac, si est qu'il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement; et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l'intestine.
The occurrence of this hernia is by the section that comes to the membrane, or the extension on the belly in the part of the groins, which is why the intestine descends from this rupture to one of the testicles; and this rupture is either of the membrane, or of its extension, and these two manners come from many causes: either from percussion, or from jumping, or from shouting, or from lifting a heavy burden, and by similar things; and the signs when it is from the extension of the membrane, is that it happens little by little, over a long time, and does not come suddenly; and the abscess is equal up to the depth, because the membrane presses the intestine. 


Et li signes est quant c'est de la section dou syfac, qu'elle fait venir a l'encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c'est por l'issue de l'intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.
And the signs when it is from the section of the membrane, is that it brings sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscess appears different, close under the skin, and this is because of the exit of the intestine and the body outside of the membrane.

Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l'intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.
And sometimes the omentum descends with the intestine, and is retained there, and causes great pain to the patient, especially when it is pressed.

Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s'en covient eschuir.
And in these iron cures there is fear, which is why it is appropriate to avoid them.

Et li maniere de l'ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu'il ramoine l'intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s'il i puet rentreir; puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes; puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc; puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;
And the manner of the procedure is that you command the patient to bring back the intestine with his hand inside the wound, if he can re-enter it; then he should be laid on his back between your hands, and raise the thighs; then extend the heart above, and cut all the skin of the testicles lengthwise; then push inside the lips of the cut hooks according to what you need to open the wound, and let it be such that the egg can come out;

puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;
then skin the membrane that is under the skin of the testicles, until the hard white membrane is uncovered on all sides;

puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l'uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l'uef, et entre lou secont syfac;
then push your index finger into what follows the testicle, into what is between the white membrane that is under the skin of the egg, and between the second membrane, and separate what is behind the egg, and between the second membrane;

et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l'uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;
and then move with the right hand inside the heart of the testicles, and extend the white membrane upwards with your left hand, and lift the egg with all the membrane towards the cut;

et comande au ministre qu'il estende l'uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;
and command the minister to extend the egg upwards, and untie what is attached behind the binding;

et quier a tes dois s'il a point de l'intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;
