and search with your fingers if there is any intestine wrapped in the hard white membrane, and if you find anything, push it into the belly below;

puis pren une aguille ou il ait .i. gros fil fait de .x. filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;
then take a needle with a thick thread made of 10 threads, and push it into the back part of the membrane, which is after the skin of the testicles;

aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu'il i ait .iiij. filz;
after the cut, then cut the ends that appear from the threads, until there are 4 threads;

puis les assemble l'un sus l'autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d'un fort liien de .ij. pars;
then assemble them one on top of the other in the manner of a cross, and tie the membrane, which we have said is under the skin of the testicles, with a strong tie of 2 parts;

puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de .ij. pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n'i viegne;
then wrap the ends of the threads, and tie them strongly in 2 parts, so that none of the vessels that nourish them can enter them, so that no hot abscess comes there;

et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc .ij. dois de celui, et aprés ces .ij. liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d'un doi;
and put again the tie according to the first tie long 2 fingers from it, and after these 2 ties leave from the membrane that is under the heart of the testicles the size of a finger;

et aprés tout l'autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;
and after all the other according to the roundness that the egg carries;

puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;
then cut in the part that is under the skin of the testicles, until the blood runs, and the pus, as we have said before;

puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.
then administer wool soaked in oil, and put in wounds, and administer the tie that we have said.

Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l'incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.
And sometimes the white membrane that we have mentioned is cauterized, after the incision, for fear of blood flow.

Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu'il chiece per lui;
For this happens many times, and leave the tie until it falls by itself;

et s'il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d'aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu'il chiece;
and if it is slow to fall, let it be sprinkled with hot water, and put on what we have said, until it falls;

puis cure la plaie d'autre cure, tant qu'il soit sanez parfaitement.
then treat the wound with other treatment, until it is perfectly healed.

de hernie carnouse
On fleshy hernia

En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.
In this hernia, I never saw anyone who dared to do the cure by iron.

Et li ancien dirent qu'ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;
And the ancients said that it is done like the hernia that is with the screw, in such a way that you tie the vessels, after the cut on them lightly below;

puis cope em mi, et cure l'aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu'il soit sanez.
then cut in the middle, and treat the abscess with what works, until the vessels fall; and treat it as we have said, until it is healed.

Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s'il en i dessent, c'est poc, et repaire toutes houres;
Sometimes a rupture comes in the groins, as we have said, and the place appears; and none of the intestines descend to the testicles, and if any descend, it is little, and returns all hours;

et toutevoie s'il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;
and yet if it remains too long at this point, the wound in the membrane grows, so that the intestine descends;

et ceu avient par l'estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;
and this happens by the extension of the membrane that is in the groins, as we have said, for it is extended, then the place is softened and swollen and appears;

et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere: et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de .iij. dois;
and the cure is by cautery, as we have said before; and sometimes it is cured by iron in this manner: and it is that the patient lies on his back between your hands, then cut the place of the swollen rupture widely according to the quantity of 3 fingers;

et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l'ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac; et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les .ij. leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l'un et l'autre;
and then extract the membrane that is under the skin that follows it, then take the ray and put it on the apparent place of the membrane; and press it to the depth of the belly, then sew the 2 apparent places of the membrane on the head of the ray, and sew one and the other;

puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n'estendre l'uef n'autre chose, si com je t'ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;
then extract the head of the ray, and do not cut any of the membrane nor extend the egg or anything else, as I have made you know in the cure of the hernia of the intestines;

puis le cure par la cure des plaies. Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu'elle soit sanee.
then treat it by the treatment of wounds. And when you cut the threads, clean it and treat the wound, until it is healed.

Li syfac est constrains, et n'a point d'apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.
The membrane is constrained, and has no appearance in the rupture, and the cautery is better in this place, and closer to health.

de l'amollissement dou cuir des coions
On the softening of the skin of the testicles

Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;
Many times the skin of the testicles is softened in some men, because the flesh that is inside is softened, and it is ugly to see;

et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c'on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;
and it is necessary, when one wants to cure it, to make the patient lie on his back, and cut the skin that is softened on the natural skin;

puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement;
then assemble the 2 lips with a suture, and if you want, sew first the superfluity of the softened skin with 3 or 4 sutures firmly;

puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu'il soit sanez, et chient li fil.
then cut between the sutures, and treat it like other wounds, until it is healed, and the threads fall.

dou chastrement
On castration

Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n'en parlasse mie en cest livre;
Know that castration is excommunicated in our law, and for this reason I would be pleased not to speak of it in this book;

et n'est necessaires fuer que por .ij. manieres: dont l'une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;
and it is not necessary except for 2 ways: one of which is that the physician knows how to respond when asked about it, and knows the cure;

et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d'aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d'autres bestes.
and the other, because we often need castration of some animals to help us, such as goat and sheep and cat and other animals.

Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc .ij. manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.
I say then that castration is done according to 2 ways: either by attraction, or by splitting.

En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;
In the one we do by attraction, we make the animal sit in hot water, until the testicles are softened and hanging;

puis les preing a ta main, tant qu'il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.
then take them in your hand, until they are gone and you no longer feel them.

 Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a .i. cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;
 On castration by cutting: it is necessary that you hold the animal, and press the skin of the testicles with your left hand, then tie the suspensory, and cut on each egg with one blow, when you have well skinned them;

et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;
and leave some of the membrane and the subtle membrane that is on the vessels;

et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l'atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;
and this manner of castration is better than that which is done by attraction, because in attraction perhaps something of the testicles remains, by which the animal desires luxury;

puis cure la plaie tant qu'ele soit sanee.
then treat the wound until it is healed.

des hermofrodites
On hermaphrodites

Hermofrodie est selonc .ij. manieres as homes: l'une si est que entre les .ij. coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d'une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.
Hermaphroditism is of two types in men: one is that between the two testicles appears something like the figure of a woman's nature, where there is hair, and sometimes urine flows from it.

 Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et .ij. coions.
 And the other type is in women, and has on the pubis something like a penis and two testicles.

 Et li cure de l'ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n'a point de cure.
 And the cure for the man and the woman is that you cut all the added flesh, and treat them like other wounds; in the second type, for men whose urine leaks through the skin of the testicles, there is no cure.

de la tentigene
On the clitoris

Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu'elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l'ont ausi grant com une main, et c'est li cure.
The clitoris is an added flesh on the natural part, so much that it is too ugly to see; and some women have it as big as a hand, and this is the cure.

Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n'aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n'i viegne, puis le cure d'autre cure tant qu'il soit sanez;
It is necessary that you hold the excess of the clitoris with your hand or with hooks, and cut it lightly; and do not go too deep, so that blood flow does not come, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed;

et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l'emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d'une kowe, et por ceu l'apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».
and there is another flesh that grows at the mouth of the womb, and fills it, and by chance protrudes out, and is like the appearance of a tail, and for this reason the ancients called it "tailed disease".

Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu'elle soit sanee.
So it is necessary that you cut it, as we have said for the clitoris, and treat it until it is healed.

de erratique
On erratic (abnormal) conditions

Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n'est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;
Erratic is when the nature of the woman is not pierced, or the hole is small; and it is natural by birth, or accidental by disease that has come there;

ou c'est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;
or it is by added flesh, or from the subtle or thick membrane, and is made deep in the womb, or on the sides, or below, or wherever;

et deffent le concevoir, et l'enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.
and it prevents conception, and childbirth, and by chance having periods; and the knowledge of this is by the midwife's examination.

Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.
If the obstruction is appearing close, search with your fingers or with the probe.

S'il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as .ij. leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes .ij. dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;
If it is from the subtle membrane, and it is close to the two lips, hurry, and break it thus: put your two index fingers together, and the woman should be on her back, with her legs spread;

puis estent les .ij. leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;
then stretch the two lips strongly, until the subtle membrane is round, and the obstruction is opened;

puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu'il ne puist souder.
then take wool, and soak it in oil, and put it on the place, and let the woman lie with a man each day, so that it cannot close.

Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.
And if the membrane is hard and thick, it is necessary that you cut it with a spatula resembling a myrtle leaf.

Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l'oncine et la cope; et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d'uef;
If the obstruction is from grown flesh, suspend it with a hook and cut it; and have blood-stopping medicines, such as acacia, dragon's blood, incense, together with egg white;

puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder; et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;
then administer a wide lead pipe, so that the wound cannot close; and let it be so for a long time, and administer a dry linen tent;

puis soit curez d'autres cures tant qu'il soit sanez.
then let it be treated with other treatments until it is healed.

Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n'est apostemes enchancrez. Car a l'aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.
And when grown flesh comes in the womb, it is necessary to cut it according to this manner, if it is not a cancerous abscess. For the cancerous abscess that is in the womb, one should not touch with iron.

des emorroides
On hemorrhoids

Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;
Hemorrhoids are openings of veins from which blood flows customarily, and when the hemorrhoids are old they become thela;

et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d'aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.
and we have already said in the division their appearances, and the signs, and I will say here those that receive treatment.

Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n'aperent au sentir, si n'est mie li cure par fer.
I say that the hemorrhoids and the thela, when they are deep in the womb, and they do not appear to the touch, the cure is not by iron.

Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c'on puet sentir, sont cil c'on puet curer.
Those that are at the mouth of the womb, that one can feel, are those that one can cure.

Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l'altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;
It is necessary then that you put the woman in a cold house, then extend the thelul with forceps, and cut it at its roots, then powder on blood-restraining medicines, such as acacia and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things;

puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide; et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d'escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses,
then push her feet to the wall for an hour, then put her in cold water; and if blood flow comes, make her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate peel and galls and similar things,

et puis pren farine d'orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai .i. emplaustre sus son dos.
and then take barley flour, and mix it with honey and vinegar, and make a plaster on her back.

Et se il estainche, c'est boin. Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;
And if it stops, that's good. If not, make her apply cupping glasses to her back and breasts without striking;

puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d'aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.
then take wool, and soak it in plantain juice or in wild rose juice with old wine, and make it adhere to the place.

Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d'oignement tant qu'il soit sanez;
And when the abscess rests, treat the place with ointment until it is healed;

et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a .i. chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j'ai dit le thelul; et puis lou cure tant qu'il soit sanez.
and that which is called "albathir" is red, and is like a rough head, so it is necessary to cut it as I have said for the thelul; and then treat it until it is healed.

des apostemes de la marris
On abscesses of the womb

Maintes manieres d'aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j'ai dit en la division.
Many types of abscesses come in the womb, such as cancer and stony abscess and herpes and gangrene and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscess, and several other diseases that I have said in the division.

Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l'aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n'est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;
It is necessary then that I speak in this treatise of the hot abscess that comes in the womb, which is not one of the abscesses that collect pus;

et se tu vues savoir l'ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l'encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s'il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.
and if you want to know the work of iron, look if the abscess is acute at the beginning of its coming, and full of heat and fever, and if it becomes red if you can see it.

Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;
Then do not hurry to pierce, but make it mature until the pain is eased;

et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus .i. siege, et ait .ij. petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;
and then make the patient sit on a seat, and have 2 small seats where she leans, and supports on her back and gathers her feet to the parts outside the leg;

et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d'un boin liien;
and let her thighs be spread, and put her arms under her knees, and tie them well with a good tie;

puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l'estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;
then the midwife sucks towards the right side, and administers the instrument with which one opens the mouth of the womb, of which the form comes hereafter;

et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l'estrument n'i viegne plus em parfont qu'il ne doit, et qu'il ne blece la malaide;
and it is necessary that when you want to administer this instrument, that you stick the probe first to know the depth of the womb, so that what enters of the instrument does not come deeper than it should, and that it does not hurt the patient;

et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;
and if the instrument is larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the womb with cloths, so that the instrument does not hurt her;

et covient qu'il mette le cornet de l'estrument au desus, et qu'il teigne l'estrument.
and it is necessary that she puts the horn of the instrument above, and that she holds the instrument.

Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;
And when the abscess appears, and one splits it with the soft hand, it is necessary to cut it at the head, with the wide spatula;

et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;
and when the pus is emptied, it is necessary that you put in the wound tents soaked in rose oil, or in dry green oil;

et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;
and put the tent out of the wound to the depth of the womb, and put outside on the womb and on the pubis clean wool soaked in water where mallows have been cooked;

puis le cure aprés .ij. jors d'oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu'il soit sanez;
then treat it after 2 days with ointment suitable for this, until it is healed;

et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d'aigue et de miel, et puis d'aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;
and sometimes one washes the womb and the wound by clyster of water and honey, and then of water where lily roots and long aristolochia have been cooked;

puis reveigne a l'oignement.
then return to the ointment.

Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.
And if the wound is hidden in the womb, it is necessary that you refrain from burning with iron, but treat it as we have said in the division.

de l'enfantement
On childbirth

Mestier est premier a la baile qu'elle conoisse la figure de l'enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l'ar: adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;
It is first necessary for the midwife that she knows the figure of natural childbirth, and the sign is when you see the woman pressing down, and desiring to smell the air: then the child hastens to come out;
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;
Then know that this childbirth is according to the natural figure, and the exit is under its head, and the afterbirth with it;

et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;
and when you see these signs, it is necessary to press lightly on her belly, so that the child comes out quickly;

car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;
for when it descends on its head, the afterbirth comes out with it, and the womb is cleansed of its superfluities by good purification;

et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.
and this one who comes otherwise does not come naturally.

Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;
For it sometimes comes on its feet, and the body or the head comes out, and the hands, or it comes on its belly, or on its back, and is turned by chance on its neck, and by other bad positions;

si est mestier a la baile qu'elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d'error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.
so it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and subtle in these things, and to beware of error and deception, and I will show you all the figures of how one should help her.

Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;
If the child comes on its head by natural exit, and the woman gives birth with difficulty, and her strength is weak, make her sit on a chair, where the women hold her;

et arose sa nature d'oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:
and sprinkle her nature with oil where fenugreek has been cooked, and then the midwife pushes between her fingers the little spatula of which this is the form:

et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;
and split the afterbirth, and cut with her nail until the moisture that is inside runs out;

et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s'il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;
and press the woman's belly until the child descends, and if it doesn't descend, it is necessary to give the woman an enema of fenugreek mucilage with sesame oil;

puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre: si istra maintenant l'enfes.
then make her push and sneeze from condisi, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour: the child will come out now.

Et se les .ij. mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;
And if the two hands come out, it is necessary that you bring them back gently little by little;

et s'elles n'i puent entrer, si met la femme sus .i. siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;
and if they cannot enter, put the woman on a seat, and raise her feet high;

puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu'elle ne chiece au deboutement;
then push the seat onto the ground, and hold the woman, so that she does not fall during the pushing;

et se li mains n'i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l'enfant, et ramoine igalment.
and if the hands cannot enter, and the child dies, cut off its hands with the knife that is placed here before, and extract the child, and bring it back evenly.

de l'issue de l'enfant sus ses piés
Of the exit of the child on its feet

Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;
When the child comes on its feet, it is necessary to push it up;

et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu'il soit igalz;
and then turn it little by little, until it is even;

puis preigne .i. des piez et l'estende poc et poc.
then take one of the feet and extend it little by little.

Cant il saut jusc'as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi; si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.
When it jumps up to the thighs, command her to push, and make her sneeze from condisi; it will jump out, if God wills.

Et s'il n'ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu'il soit selonc la figure natureil.
And if it doesn't come out as we have said, turn it little by little, until it is according to the natural figure.

Car adonques ist il legierement.
For then it comes out easily.

Et s'il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en .i. mortier;
And if it doesn't come out as we have said, take marshmallow mucilage, and sesame oil, and melted gum, and grind everything in a mortar;

et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;
and put this ointment on the woman's nature inside and outside, then make her sit in lukewarm water up to below the ribs;

et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai .i. coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;
and when she is softened below, make her a collar of myrrh, and put it underneath, and leave it for an hour;

puis la fai seoir sus .i. siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.
then make her sit on a seat, then make her sneeze and tighten her mouth and nose, and press her belly lightly, for the child jumps out now.

de l'issue de l'enfant sus ses genous
Of the exit of the child on its knees

Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;
When the child comes in this form, let the midwife put her hands little by little;

puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor .i. lit;
then let her be laid on her neck, and her feet hanging down, and lying on a bed;

et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu'elle soit appareillie aval;
and fold her hands little by little, and then press her hands on the belly, and remove the cushions from underneath, until she is prepared below;

et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;
and if the child doesn't jump, take its feet and move them strongly, then move the belly upwards, then push your hands;

et ewe l'enfant poc et poc; et comande a la femme qu'elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.
and deliver the child little by little; and command the woman to push until the child comes out.

de l'issue de l'enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant
Of the exit of the child who comes with one hand hanging out

I covient engignier a ramener la main: s'on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;
It is necessary to contrive to bring back the hand: if one cannot bring it back, make the woman get up and walk;

s'elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus .i. lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;
if she cannot walk, make her lie on a bed, and push her legs strongly;

puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j'ai conteit; et s'elle n'enfante, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;
then administer the mucilage that I have told; and if she doesn't give birth, make her sit on a seat, then study to bring back the hand;

et ewe l'enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu'elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.
and deliver the child according to the natural figure, and make her sneeze, and command her to push until the child comes out.

de l'issue de l'enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere
Of the exit of the child on its neck, with its hands spread out, and its face turned towards its mother's back

I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l'ewe legierement;
It is necessary that the midwife hold her hand, then turn it little by little, and deliver it lightly;

et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu'elle se mueve poc et poc;
and when it is even, put marshmallow mucilage and oil on the nature, as we have said, then command her to move little by little;

et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, et li comande k'elle se preigne; et la fai esternuer.
and when you have done this, make her sit on a seat, and command her to push; and make her sneeze.

de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine
Of this same manner with all the afterbirth

Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;
When it comes out in this manner with all the afterbirth, cut the afterbirth with your nail, until the moisture is emptied;

et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu'elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;
and if the child hangs on its face and on its neck, cut it from the navel, so that it is not retained, and the child dies;

puis boute l'enfant dedens, tant que tu l'aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu'elle se preigne aucune fois: adonques si istra legierement.
then push the child inside, until you have put it as it should be, and command the woman to push sometimes: then it will come out easily.

de l'issue des gemelz
Of the exit of twins

Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent .iij. ou .iiij.; et ceu n'est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.
Know that twins are born many times, and sometimes three or four are born; and this is not a strange thing, and happens rarely.

Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom; je sai ceu, qu'il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;
Two are a strange thing, and do not live, if rarely; I know this, that they are multiplied, and are separated by the membrane that divides them, which is tied to the navel;

et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.
and sometimes they come out as naturally as a single one, as we have said.

Et s'il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu'elle fait;
And if they come out with difficulty, cure her as we have said, and let the midwife be subtle, and do quickly and lightly what she does;

et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.
and do thus as it is better for health.

de plusors enfans
Of multiple children

Aucune fois sont formez en la marris .i. ou .ij. ou .iij. ou .iiij. ou .v. ou .vj. ou .vij., ou plusors jusc'a .xv., et sont tout formeit en forme d'enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient; si faice selonc ceu qu'il covient.
Sometimes one or two or three or four or five or six or seven, or more up to fifteen, are formed in the womb, and all are formed in the shape of a child by the measurement of the glorious wise one, and it is necessary that the midwife know all this, for by chance a similar thing may happen to her; so she should act according to what is necessary.

de l'enfant mort
Of the dead child

Quant tu cures la femme de l'enfant mort ou ventre, si com j'ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d'ovraige de mains;
When you treat the woman for a dead child in the womb, as I have said in the division, and it does not come out, and you are constrained to work with your hands;

si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n'ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;
it is necessary that you know if the woman is of sound strength, and has no condition where she fears death;

si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;
it is necessary that the woman be laid on her back, with her head inclined downward, and her legs raised;

et li ministre la teigne de .ij. pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu'elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l'enfant;
and the assistant should hold her on two sides, or she should be tied to the bed so that she is not pulled during the descent of the child;

puis frotez la bouche de la marris d'oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;
then rub the mouth of the womb with moist oils with mucilage of marshmallow and fenugreek and linseed, then the midwife should anoint her hands with these oils and these mucilages;

puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere .i. leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu'il dessende sus son chief;
then push them into the womb gently, then seek a place where she can push the hooks that are suitable for this, and take care if the child is prepared to descend on its head;

si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;
so fix the hooks in its eyes or in its neck or in its mouth or in its palate or under the chin or in the chest or near the ribs, and if the descent is on the feet, fix them in the groin and at the middle ribs;

et covient qu'il teigne l'oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l'oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu'il viegne a la chose vuide; et c'est li forme de l'oncine:
and it is necessary that she hold the hook with her right hand, and put the curve between the fingers of her left hand, and push it with all her hand gently, and fix the hook in one of these places that we have said, until it comes to the empty thing; and this is the form of the hook:

puis fiche encontre .i. autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;
then fix against it another hook, or the third if you need it, so that the extraction is even;

et puis l'estent igalment en movant d'une part et d'autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:
and then extend it evenly by moving from one side to the other, to come out better, and let the hooks be toothed to hold better, as is the form here:

Et s'il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d'oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l'autre partie;
And if a part remains, let the midwife anoint some of her fingers with oil, and push them into that part, and pull the other part;

et s'il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu'il s'en isse tout fuers.
and if any remains, put this hook in the highest place, and do this until it all comes out.

Et se l'une mains vient devant l'autre, et il ne puet ramener por l'estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus .i. drapeil, tant qu'il isse tote;
And if one hand comes before the other, and it cannot be brought back because of the tightness, it is necessary that you wrap it in a cloth, until it all comes out;

puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l'autre main, et as .ij. piés.
then cut it at the joint of the sole or at the elbow, and so it is necessary that you do the same to the other hand, and to the two feet.

Et se li chiés de l'enfant est gros et il est estrois en l'issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l'aigue;
And if the child's head is big and it is narrow at the exit, or if there is water gathered in the head, it is necessary that you push the spiny spatula between your fingers, and split the head and extract the water;

ou tu la ront a l'estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;
or you break it with the instrument which is called "almidach", of which the form comes with the instruments in the chapter which is after this one;

et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment; et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;
and do the same if the child has a naturally big head; and then pull out the bones with forceps, and if the head jumps out and it tightens at the chest, let it be split, until the moisture that is in the chest comes out;

et s'elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;
and if it cannot come out, cut it into pieces as best you can;

et s'il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.
and if it is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, it is necessary that you pierce it until the moisture runs.

Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.
And if the child is on its feet, the attraction is easy, and the straightening to the mouth of the womb is easy.

Et s'il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l'estraies a .i. drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;
And if it is narrow in the belly or in the chest, it is necessary that you extract it with a cloth wrapped over your hand;

et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre; et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc'a la bouche de la marris;
and split the belly or the chest, until the moisture that is there runs; and if the other limbs are removed, and the head remains, let the midwife push her hand deep into the womb, and pull it to the mouth of the womb;

puis i boute .i. oncine ou ij., et le trai fuer; et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n'i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;
then push in one or two hooks, and pull it out; and if the mouth of the womb is narrowed because of a hot abscess that has come there, it is not necessary to labor, but it is necessary to administer moist and fatty things;

et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.
and administer plasters to her, and let her sit in softening and moistening water.

Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l'enfant vif;
And if the child is on its side, and you can make it even, administer what we have said for the living child;

et s'on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n'i laissier rien de la secondine.
and if one does not have the power, pull it out in pieces, and do not leave any of the afterbirth.

Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;
And when you have done this, administer to her what we have said for hot abscesses that come in the womb;

et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.
and if a flow of blood comes, let her be put in astringent water, and administer other treatments to her.

Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.
And I saw a woman in whose belly a child had been dead, then she conceived another on top of that one, and the other was dead again.

Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu'il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.
After a long time an abscess came to her in the navel, and swelled so much that it opened, and began to have great putrefaction.

je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.
I was called to treat it, and I thought about it for a long time, and could not heal the wound.

Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.
I put on a plaster of strong attraction, and a bone came out, and after some days another.

Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c'ou ventre n'a point d'os.
I marveled greatly, because there are no bones in the belly.

Si pensai que c'estoit des os d'un enfant mort.
So I thought that it was the bones of a dead child.

Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;
I examined the wound, and pulled out many bones, until the woman was in a better state;

et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;
and the woman lived for a long time like this, and a little pus always came out of the place;

et je n'ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu'il i saiche mettre aide.
and I have recorded this chapter only so that, when the master finds a strange thing, he may know how to provide help.

dou ramener la marris a son leu
Of returning the womb to its place

Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.
Here follows the form of the press, with which one delivers the children; and it has two turnings at the two ends of the two bands.

Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;
However, let the horns be more subtle than the restrictor, and be made of ebony or boxwood;

et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;
and let the mouth of the wood be one finger wide, and the margin of the trees one finger, and one and a half palms long;

et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l'un et en l'autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;
and in the middle of the two bands let there be two adjustments of this same wood, which are fixed in one and the other, half a palm long or a little more;

et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.
and these two adjustments are pushed into the mouth of the womb to open it when one turns the two horns.

Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;
Another form, more subtle and lighter in its appearance, should be made of ebony or boxwood, in the likeness of forceps;

et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d'une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;
and let it have at the two ends two adjustments, as you see, one palm long, and two fingers wide;

et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l'estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l'estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;
and when you want to open the womb with the instrument, make the woman sit on a bed, with her feet hanging and her legs open, then push the two adjustments joined together into the womb, and hold the head of the instrument below between her thighs;

puis oevre ta main a tout l'estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu'elle vuet.
then open your hand with the whole instrument, as you have done with the forceps equally, according to the quantity that you want to open the mouth of the womb, until the midwife does what she wants.

Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.
These instruments are all surpassed, and their likenesses are multiplied; and when the physician has prepared them, the work is more hasty, and higher for men because of their quantity.

Si ne despire mie l'estrument que tu ne l'aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n'est mie escusauble.
So do not despise the instrument that you have not prepared, for their necessity is not excusable.

Quant li secondine est retenue a l'enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu'ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis; et s'elle saut per ceu, bien est.
When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, it is necessary that you command the patient to hold her breath, and then make her sneeze with condisi, and press your hands to her mouth and nose; and if it comes out because of this, it is good.

Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire; toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d'eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;
If not, then take a pot, and make a hole in the lid, and put in herbs that can open the mouth of the womb, such as calamint, rue, anise, chamomile, cassia, and centaury; all these herbs, or some of them, should be cooked in the pot with water over the fire;

puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l'autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.

then put a reed in the hole of the pot, and the other end in the mouth of the womb, and hold it until the vapors enter the womb; then make her sneeze, as we have said.

Si saut li secondine hastanment. Et s'elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n'ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu'ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;

If the afterbirth comes out quickly. And if it remains after this treatment, and does not come out, then command the midwife to wet her left hand in sesame oil or marshmallow mucilage, and then insert it into the vagina, and search for the afterbirth;

et quant elle l'avra trovee, si la preigne et l'estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l'estraction; mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.

and when she has found it, she should take it and extend it little by little directly, so that the womb does not fall during extraction; but it should be moved gently to the right and left, and then pulled; it will come and detach itself.

Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d'esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes; et s'elle n'ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;

And if the mouth of the womb is already narrowed, we have mentioned the treatment of sneezing, and fumigation with herbs; and if it does not come out with all that we have said, be careful not to be foolish in pulling;

mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d'oignement tetrafarmaçon; si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;

but it is necessary that what is at the mouth of the womb, you tie it to the woman's thigh, then give her an enema with tetrapharmacon ointment; it will rot and come out, and will come out;

mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide. Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.

but nevertheless, when it rots, a bad odor comes to the stomach and head, and harms the patient. So suitable fumigations are necessary for this: some of the ancients have tried fumigation with watercress and dried figs.

Li forme de l'estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:

The form of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman for the retention of menses and afterbirth is this:

Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu; et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu'elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.
And it is made of glass resembling a reed, and one puts the thin end in the vagina, and the wide ends over the fire; and the fumigation should be over coals, and hold it until it is used up, and start another one.

de percier lou fondement
Maint enfant naissent qui n'ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l'ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac: si covient donques a la baile qu'ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu'elle ne le touche;

On piercing the anus
Many children are born without a pierced anus, but rather it is blocked by a thin membrane: so it is necessary for the midwife to pierce this membrane with her finger, and not to pierce it with a sharp spatula, and be careful not to touch the sphincter;

puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d'oignement tant qu'il soit sanez. Et se tu doutes qu'il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.

then put wool soaked in wine and oil on it, then treat it with ointment until it is healed. And if you fear it might close up again, put a lead tube in the opening, and leave it for several days, and remove it when the child wants to go to the toilet.

Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d'aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.

And sometimes this blockage comes from the healing of a wound or abscess; so it is necessary to cut this healing: it should be treated, as we have said about the lead tube.

de la fistule dou fondement
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l'espaice des .ij. parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;

On fistulas of the anus
Fistulas that come under the anus are nodules, and swellings that come near the outside of the anus, or in the space between the two parts, so there is one fistula or several;

et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu'il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.

and when this nodule is old, it opens, and discharges watery white moisture or thin pus, and sometimes these fistulas are penetrating; and they are known by the fact that stool or gas comes out of them when the patient defecates, and perhaps a worm comes out.

Et si a fistules que percent jusc'a la vessie, et jusc'a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc'a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc'a nout de la kowe.

And there are fistulas that penetrate to the bladder, and to the middle of the penis; and reach to the hip joint, and to the tailbone.

Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant: et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d'arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n'i a tortuositeit.

And thus one knows the penetrating fistula of the anus, and the non-penetrating: it is that you put your index finger in the anus, and put a thin needle of brass or iron in the fistula when there is no tortuosity.

Et s'il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit; et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit: saiches qu'elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.

And if there is tortuosity, put in a thin lead probe, or a horse hair, until you feel the probe or the hair with your finger; and if you don't feel it, and no stool, gas or worm comes out of the opening, as we have said: know that it does not penetrate; so hasten to treat it.

Et quant li fistule est persans jusc'a la vessie ou jusc'a conduit de l'urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines. S'elle est percie jusc'a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc'au leu; s'il n'i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu'il en ist adés bowe, et n'i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;

And when the fistula penetrates to the bladder or to the urethra, urine comes out of it, and it cannot be healed by medicines. If it penetrates to the hip joint, the probe reaches to that place; if there is no tortuosity and the discovery of pain around, it is that pus always comes out of it, and medicine or healing by ointment is of no use;

et en ces fistules persans n'a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s'en entremettent. En celle qui n'est mie persans et n'est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j'ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;

and for these penetrating fistulas there is no cure except labor, and the vanity of foolish doctors who meddle with them. For those that are not penetrating and are not old, there is hope of healing by iron, as I have tested, and it is that the patient lies on his back between your hands; and lift his legs up to his thighs, and have his thighs inclined to his belly;

puis boute une tente d'arain, ou de plonc s'il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient. Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l'ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu'elle est persans; si n'i travillier mie c'on ne la puet saner.

then insert a brass probe, or a lead one if there is tortuosity, until you know where the probe comes. If the patient feels it around the anus, you should insert your index finger, if you then feel that the probe has penetrated it; and let it be uncovered where you feel between your finger the membrane or the flesh, then know that it is penetrating; so do not work on it because it cannot be healed.

On dist toutevoie c'on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc; et li aide c'on i fait, si est c'on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit; et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu'il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d'oiseil;

It is said however that some can be healed, but this happens rarely; and the help that is done, is that one heats the thin cautery according to the width of the fistula, as said before; and insert it hot into the fistula, until it comes near the anus; and do this 2 or 3 times, until you know that these felted flesh are burned, which are similar to a bird's feather;

et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d'oignement enjanrant char et soudant. S'il est ensi sanez, c'est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;

and then treat it with probes moistened in butter, until that flesh comes out, then treat it with ointment generating flesh and healing. If it is thus healed, it is good. If not, it cannot be healed otherwise;

et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc'au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur; si le cope des l'encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu'il viegne au chief de la tente; et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;

and if the probe enters, and does not penetrate to the finger that is in the anus, and there is between your finger and the probe a thick covering of flesh or membrane, and you see the fistula following the covering of the skin; so cut it from the beginning of the fistula, and keep pushing the probe forward, and then the cautery after, until it comes to the head of the probe; and the probe will be freed, and will fall;

puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d'oisel, et n'en remaigne niant. Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l'uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague. Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c'est a savoir, l'arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l'esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;

then clean those felted flesh that resemble a bird's feather, and let none remain. And if blood overcomes you, and runs between you and the work, cauterize it with fire or sharp medicine. For the cautery of fire combines two good things: namely, the burning of these added flesh, and the stopping of blood and the drying of moisture;

puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe; puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches. Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.

then treat it with probes moistened in butter or in crushed cabbage, until the place discharges pus, and the burned flesh comes out in the pus; then treat the wound with healing ointments generating hard flesh, and the medicines are dry. For when it is restored, it is healed and does not come back.

Et se fistule vient jusc'a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu. Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n'i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d'esperance, par l'aministrement de l'une des .iii. manieres: ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc'a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;

And if the fistula comes to the deep part of the anus, and is far from the body, insert your finger into the anus, and investigate this. If you feel the probe, and between the two is the cloth or the membrane or flesh, or it is close to piercing, there is only a way of confidence and hope, by the administration of one of the three ways: either you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it to the bottom, or if you can, put probes and treat as before;

et n'aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit; puis le cure, si com nos avons dit; par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu'elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;

and do not go too deep, that you do not cut the tendon that holds the anus, and the stools come out without will; then treat it, as we have said; perhaps it will be healed, or you remove that covering and clean it after it is cut near the anus, either by probe or by other pointed instrument;

puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues; puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide. Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:

then clean that felted flesh that is in the wound, as much as you can; then study to restore the wound, and to keep the fistula in the part outside the anus: it will be easier for the patient. And sometimes fistulas are like this: it is when you put the probe in the fistula, and it is on the side of the anus near the skin above, so take a probe pierced at the head according to this form:

Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu'il soit au chief. S'elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement; et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l'un a l'autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;

And put a twisted thread in two, and push the probe with all the thread into the fistula until it is at the head. If it is penetrating in the inner margin of the anus, then pull the thread from that hole, so that you put your finger in the anus; and pull the head of the thread, and bring the two ends together, and tighten one to the other, and leave it for a day or two;

et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent; puis cure la plaie tant qu'elle soit soudee et sanee. Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s'ele n'est trop em parfont. Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu'il soit sanez.

and tighten it sometimes, until the thread cuts the flesh that is between the two, and they fall; then treat the wound until it is healed and cured. If the fistula does not penetrate, make it penetrate in all the ways that you can, if it is not too deep. For it is not necessary to cut so deep for the binding, and then treat it, as we have said, until it is healed.

Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d'une, part et trenchans; et d'autre part non, por ceu c'on ne cope mie ceu c'on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:

The form of the spiny spatula with which one splits the fistula is very sharp on one side and cutting; and not on the other side, so that one does not cut what one should not cut, as you see here:

des emorroydes
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s'en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s'en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;

On hemorrhoids
Hemorrhoids are of two types: either they are inside the anus, like grapes, and there are small and large ones, and blood always flows from them, and there are one or several, and they are outside the anus and at

mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d'aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;
But those that are outside have little moisture, and always contain a little citrine water or a little blood, and have the color of the body;

et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu'il s'espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c'aperent li filz;
And the cure for those who have them inside the anus is that you command the patient to strain to go to the toilet, until the anus comes out, and the threads appear;

si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;
So hurry, and grab it with tweezers, or hold it with your nail, then cut it at its roots;

et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d'une piece de chamelot;
And if the hook cannot hold them because of their moisture, take them with a cloth, or cotton, or a piece of camelot;

et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;
And pull them with your fingers, then cut them, and powder them with some hot powders that serve as cautery;

ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d'autres cures tant qu'il soit sanez;
Or cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cautery, then treat them with other cures until they are healed;

et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu'il puist issir apertement;
And if the anus cannot come out, give the patient an enema with a biting and harsh clyster to wash what is in the anus, so that it can come out openly;

cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;
When the patient strains, and if the threads are outside the anus, the cure is easy;

et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu'il soit sanez, et qu'il redoute l'incision par fer.
And it is that you take them with your nail or with tweezers, and cut them, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed, and that he fears incision by iron.

Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l'aguille d'autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l'aguille, et si soit dou large;
So it is necessary that you administer the suture in this manner: take a twisted thread, and push it into a needle, and then pull the thread above and make the needle pierce the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread under the needle, and let it be wide;

et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l'aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;
And tighten the thread strongly, then tie the thread, and pull out the needle, and do this for all the others, and leave one to drain the excess blood;

puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k'il repose;
Then put on the anus a cloth soaked in rose oil or in cerate, and put it on the anus, and command the patient to rest;

et puis le laisse tant qu'il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d'oignement et d'autre cure, tant qu'il soit sanez.
And then leave it until they fall, and when they have fallen, treat them with ointment and other cures, until they are healed.

dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement
On the drying of feces in the anus

Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l'intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n'i vaut.
Many times drying of feces occurs in the intestine, and by constraint of nature, and when the disease is old and medicine is of no use.

Si covient que tu reses a la point d'un spatumile ou a ton ungle l'escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;
So it is necessary that you scrape with the point of a spatula or with your nail the crust above, which does not allow it to moisten;

puis le cure tant qu'il soit sodez si com il covient; et s'il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu'il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;
Then treat it until it is soldered as it should be; and if it cannot solder, start the scraping stronger than before, until it bleeds a lot, and is skinned;

puis le cure tant qu'il soit sanez.
Then treat it until it is healed.

dou fremit
On the ant (possibly referring to a skin condition)

Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;
Formice is a small felted appearance around the body, and goes very deep;

et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.
And sometimes the cold finds it, and one feels it like the bite of an ant, and it comes in all the body, and more in the hands than elsewhere.

Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d'une penne d'oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;
And the cure is that you take a quill of a goose feather, or a strong vulture feather, and put this quill on the ant, until the circle encompasses the ant all around;

puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.
Then turn your hand with the quill until you cut all around the ant, and put it deep, and uproot the ant from its roots.

Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d'une caine d'arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:
And if you want, do this with a brass or iron tube according to this shape, and let it be thin below and pulling above:

ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.
Not pierced, to better hold with the finger, and better press And if you want, cauterize the ant, as it is mentioned before in the chapter on cautery.

de la forme dou clistere
On the shape of the clyster

Aucune fois fait on clistere d'argent ou d'archaut, ou d'arain fondut ou mailliet;
Sometimes one makes a clyster of silver or of brass, or of molten or hammered copper;

et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.
And sometimes one makes these instruments small and large, according to those to whom they are administered.

Cil donques c'on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.
Those therefore that one administers in the treatment of children and who are weak and in pain, are small.

Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:
The shape of the small and large clyster is wide above, where the belly is tied in this manner:

et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;
And there is a separation where the belly is tied, as you see, and the head is pierced inside;

et ait a l'un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l'autre .i.; et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d'une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d'espaice,
And it has on one side two holes, and on the other one; and let the belly where one puts the medicines be of an animal bladder or parchment, and be pierced all around with small holes, and have between each hole a finger's space,

puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;
Then push into these holes a strong thread of raw twisted thread in 10 or thereabouts, and assemble the belly as is a goat;

et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l'estrument devant d'un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c'est li forme dou cercle:
And when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument in front with a strong thread, then give the enema; and this is the shape of the circle:

Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d'oile ou d'aubun d'uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;
And let the medicine be neither too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the clyster with oil or egg white, or similar thing, then push it in gently;

puis l'espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu'il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,
Then let the minister squeeze it with his two hands together, until it is all empty, then pull out the clyster, and let the patient raise his legs against the wall,

et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s'il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.
And if the medicine wants to come out, let him hold it as long as he can; and if he sleeps a night with it all, it is of greater help.

Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d'issir, si le rencomence tant qu'il soit sanez.
And if you give him an enema in a disease of diarrhea, and the medicine hastens to come out, start again until he is healed.

Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant; et c'est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:
And if there are hemorrhoids in the anus, or an abscess, let the clyster be as thin as for a child; and this is the shape of the thin clyster on which the skin should be tightened:

des plaies
On wounds

Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l'acomplissement.
We have already said in the division the cure of wounds; now we will tell you the cures of hands and medicine, according to the accomplishment.

Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu'elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.
I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and of what they are made.

Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d'espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;
The things by which wounds are made are by throwing of stone, and cut of sword and knife, or of lance or of wood or of arrow, or of similar things;

ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;
Or that are made according to the places of the body, such as wound that falls on the neck, or on the head, or the chest, or the belly, or the liver, and similar members;

et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.
And I will tell you the cure for each wound, and will begin with simple head wounds, for the remembrance will come in its chapter.

Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n'est brisiez, si pren garde se c'est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d'aposteme chaut:
I say that when a simple wound comes to the head, and the bone is not broken, take care if it is from throwing of stone or similar things, and the skin is nevertheless broken and the wound is large, and you fear the raising of a hot abscess:

si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s'il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;
So make it bleed immediately from the cephalic vein especially if little blood comes from the wound, and let the bleeding be on the opposite side of the wounded part;

et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.
And let the patient avoid repletion of wine and heavy foods.

Et s'il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;
And if he does not want to bleed, let his food be reduced, and let him not drink wine, nor eat meat;

et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;
And put on the wound, if a hot abscess comes, cotton soaked in rose oil only, or in styptic wine;

et s'il n'i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s'elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n'est muee par l'air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;
And if there is no hot abscess, put on the wound, if it is fresh with all its blood, and it is not changed by the air, powder, which I will tell about a little later;

et se li ars l'ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu'il soit sanez.
And if the air has changed it, put some ointments on it, until it is healed.

Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d'espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.
And if the wound is large as from a sword cut and similar, and the lips cannot be assembled by tents, assemble them by suture, as I will say for wounds of the belly, about the suture.

Se li plaie est descoverte de l'os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;
If the wound is uncovered from the bone, and hangs, and holds only by a little, cut it;
